      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Law_of_4_February_1794">Law of 4 February 1794</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FLaw_of_4_February_1794&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Law_of_4_February_1794&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that <b><a href="/wiki/Law_of_4_February_1794" title="Law of 4 February 1794">the first law abolishing slavery in French colonies</a></b> passed unopposed after a delegate exclaimed that a long debate would dishonor the <a href="/wiki/National_Convention" title="National Convention">National Convention</a>? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/ASPC0001973700/page/n49/mode/2up">[32]</a></small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that while France <b><a href="/wiki/Law_of_4_February_1794" title="Law of 4 February 1794">first abolished slavery in 1794</a></b>, it was reinstated in 1802? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://hdl.handle.net/2027%2Fheb.03158">[33]</a></small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: N/A (only second DYK)</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>

      <h4><span id="Marja_Kuba.C5.A1ec"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Marja_Kubašec">Marja Kubašec</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FMarja_Kuba%C5%A1ec&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Marja_Kuba%C5%A1ec&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 122px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Kubasec_Marja_SKA_NII_1B_Wupokaz_CSR_001.jpg" class="image" title="Portrait of Marja Kubašec in c. 1930"><img alt="Portrait of Marja Kubašec in c. 1930" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Kubasec_Marja_SKA_NII_1B_Wupokaz_CSR_001.jpg/122px-Kubasec_Marja_SKA_NII_1B_Wupokaz_CSR_001.jpg" decoding="async" width="122" height="160" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Kubasec_Marja_SKA_NII_1B_Wupokaz_CSR_001.jpg/183px-Kubasec_Marja_SKA_NII_1B_Wupokaz_CSR_001.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Kubasec_Marja_SKA_NII_1B_Wupokaz_CSR_001.jpg/244px-Kubasec_Marja_SKA_NII_1B_Wupokaz_CSR_001.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3078" data-file-height="4042"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Portrait of Marja Kubašec in <abbr title="circa">c.</abbr> 1930
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that <b><a href="/wiki/Marja_Kuba%C5%A1ec" title="Marja Kubašec">Marja Kubašec</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> was both the first <a href="/wiki/Sorbs" title="Sorbs">Sorbian</a> woman to receive a formal teacher training and the first woman to write a novel in <a href="/wiki/Upper_Sorbian" title="Upper Sorbian">Upper Sorbian</a>? <small>Source: For the teacher training: "Als erste ausgebildete sorbische Lehrerin verfasste [K]ubašec ..." Scholze (2007). For the woman to write a novel in Upper Sorbian: "Kubašec's significance as the first woman novelist in Upper-Lusatian-Sorbian is clear ..." <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.co.uk/books?id=2Wf1SVbGFg8C&amp;printsec=frontcover&amp;source=gbs_ge_summary_r&amp;cad=0#v=onepage&amp;q&amp;f=false">Wilson</a> (1991) 674.</small></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Bambusa_blumeana" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Bambusa blumeana">Bambusa blumeana</a></li>

      <h3><span id="Articles_created.2Fexpanded_on_May_31"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Articles_created/expanded_on_May_31">Articles created/expanded on May 31</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know/Approved&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Articles created/expanded on May 31">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="WVSS">WVSS</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FWVSS&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=WVSS&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <p><s>* ... that the manager of <b><a href="/wiki/WVSS" title="WVSS">WVSS</a></b> at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Wisconsin%E2%80%93Stout" title="University of Wisconsin–Stout">University of Wisconsin–Stout</a> spent $6,000 of his own money to buy more than 500 classical music CDs to program the station?</s> </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><b>ALT1</b>: ... that the manager of <b><a href="/wiki/WVSS" title="WVSS">WVSS</a></b> at the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Wisconsin%E2%80%93Stout" title="University of Wisconsin–Stout">University of Wisconsin–Stout</a> spent about $6,000 of his own money to buy more than 500 classical music CDs to program the station? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://www.newspapers.com/clip/78692116/">https://www.newspapers.com/clip/78692116/</a></small></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Schools_at_War" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Schools at War">Template:Did you know nominations/Schools at War</a></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <p><small>5x expanded by <a href="/wiki/User:Sammi_Brie" title="User:Sammi Brie">Sammi Brie</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Sammi_Brie" title="User talk:Sammi Brie">talk</a>). Self-nominated at 23:09, 31 May 2021 (UTC).</small> </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li class="mw-empty-elt"></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <p>I don't have time to do a full review, but I will do a thorough check tomorrow of verificiation/copyright/neutrality. Otherwise, article was expanded within the last 7 days of nomination (363 bytes -&gt; 2003 bytes), longer than 1500 bytes, has an interesting hook, hook is less than 200 characters and QPQ is provided. Rest of the review will come tomorrow&nbsp;:) --<a href="/wiki/User:MrLinkinPark333" title="User:MrLinkinPark333">MrLinkinPark333</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MrLinkinPark333" title="User talk:MrLinkinPark333">talk</a>) 03:43, 1 June 2021 (UTC) </p> 
      <ul>
       <li><a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_possible_vote.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol possible vote.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Symbol_possible_vote.svg/16px-Symbol_possible_vote.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Symbol_possible_vote.svg/24px-Symbol_possible_vote.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/ca/Symbol_possible_vote.svg/32px-Symbol_possible_vote.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> Checking through this article, I have a list of issues that need addressing for fixing. Most are verification issues.</li> 
       <li>"a <b>university</b> committee had been researching the idea of a station" - suggest dropping the word university as Stoutonia doesn't mention the type of committee. You also stated Stout State was a university earlier in the sentence, so it's redundant.<img alt="check" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/20px-Yes_check.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="20" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/30px-Yes_check.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/40px-Yes_check.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600"><span style="display:none">Y</span></li> 
       <li>"WVSS went on air in the fall of 1970, <b>initially</b> operating for seven hours a day." - Original Research issue with the word "initially". It suggests that the radio station started at seven hours a day, then later changed. However, The Dunn County News doesn't specify a change in hours, only that it was on air for 7 hours weekly when it started in 1970. Either a source is needed to show the change of hours (if that is the case), or the word "initially" can be dropped for accuracy.<img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/18px-X_mark.svg.png" decoding="async" width="18" height="21" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/27px-X_mark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/36px-X_mark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="525" data-file-height="600"> <b>Not done</b></li> 
       <li>"The studios were located in the former Central Elementary School" - Original Research issue as Stoutonia 1968 was written before the 1970 launch. This also contradicts with The Dunn County News which says it was held in Stout State's communications basement. It could be the same place, but a source would be needed to show that the Central Elementary School became the Stout State University's school of communications. Otherwise, you could swap this out with what The Dunn County News says in 1970.<img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/18px-X_mark.svg.png" decoding="async" width="18" height="21" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/27px-X_mark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/36px-X_mark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="525" data-file-height="600"> <b>Not done</b></li> 
       <li>"Broadcasts were upgraded to stereo in December 1975" - Similar issue. Stoutonia 1975 was written before the upgrade was to happen. Either a source is needed to show that it did happen in December 1975, or the sentence would need rewriting to state that it was scheduled to happen then.<img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/18px-X_mark.svg.png" decoding="async" width="18" height="21" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/27px-X_mark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/36px-X_mark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="525" data-file-height="600"> <b>Not done</b></li> 
       <li>"student programming from UW–Stout moved to a cable system as "C-Rock"" - Yes. However, only Stoutonia 1989 mentions C-Rock, and not The Leader-Telegram 1988. Either the entire sentence can be bundled with the two citations, or the C-Rock part can be cited with Stoutonia 1989.<img alt="check" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/20px-Yes_check.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="20" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/30px-Yes_check.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/40px-Yes_check.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600"><span style="display:none">Y</span> 
        <ul>
         <li>"accept advertising from local businesses" - word for word copy of The Leader-Telegram 1988. I suggest a slight reword to pass limited wording.<img alt="check" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/20px-Yes_check.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="20" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/30px-Yes_check.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/40px-Yes_check.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600"><span style="display:none">Y</span> 
          <ul>
           <li>Nice rewording! --<a href="/wiki/User:MrLinkinPark333" title="User:MrLinkinPark333">MrLinkinPark333</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MrLinkinPark333" title="User talk:MrLinkinPark333">talk</a>) 00:39, 2 June 2021 (UTC)</li>
          </ul></li>
        </ul></li> 
       <li>"The station <b>manager</b>, Arthur "Ace" Matthews," - The Dunn County News 1988 says he's general manager of the station, not manager.<img alt="check" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/20px-Yes_check.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="20" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/30px-Yes_check.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/40px-Yes_check.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600"><span style="display:none">Y</span> 
        <ul>
         <li>"Matthews spent <b>$6,000</b> of his own money on a collection of <b>some</b> 540 classical music CDs" - almost correct. The Dunn County News 1988 said it was exactly 540 CDs, totally around $6,000, but not exactly $6,000.<img alt="check" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/20px-Yes_check.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="20" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/30px-Yes_check.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/40px-Yes_check.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600"><span style="display:none">Y</span></li>
        </ul></li> 
       <li>Per above, the hook is inaccurate with <b>$6,000</b>. Should be around $6,000, not exactly $6,000.<img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/18px-X_mark.svg.png" decoding="async" width="18" height="21" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/27px-X_mark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/36px-X_mark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="525" data-file-height="600"> <b>Not done</b></li> 
       <li>"went silent for seven months in the <b>spring</b> of 1990" Per <a href="/wiki/MOS:SEASON" class="mw-redirect" title="MOS:SEASON">MOS:SEASON</a>, spring should be swapped/dropped. Either you could state when they went off the air or when they came back.<img alt="check" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/20px-Yes_check.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="20" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/30px-Yes_check.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/40px-Yes_check.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600"><span style="display:none">Y</span></li> 
       <li>"The changes came at a time when WPR was restructuring into two program services but only had one transmitter to cover western Wisconsin" - Original Research as this is from The Leader-Telegram 1988, while WVSS was still on the air before the 7-month silence in 1990. The article does mention that WVSS had swapped over to cable rock &amp; classical music, so this part could be reorganized there. However, see next point below.<img alt="check" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/20px-Yes_check.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="20" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/30px-Yes_check.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/40px-Yes_check.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600"><span style="display:none">Y</span> 
        <ul>
         <li>Also, the article talks about a possibility about making two radio stations, but that hadn't happened yet, making this Original Research too.<img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/64/Purple_question_mark.svg/18px-Purple_question_mark.svg.png" decoding="async" width="18" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/64/Purple_question_mark.svg/27px-Purple_question_mark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/64/Purple_question_mark.svg/36px-Purple_question_mark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="450" data-file-height="450"> <b>Not sure</b></li>
        </ul></li> 
       <li>"The site change was mutually exclusive with an application by WVCY" - sorta. 1995 Leader-Telegram says Wisconsin Voice of Christian Youth filed the application. While they own WVCY, 1995 Leader-Telegram doesn't specifically state WVCY was the filing station.<img alt="check" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/20px-Yes_check.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="20" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/30px-Yes_check.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/fb/Yes_check.svg/40px-Yes_check.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="600"><span style="display:none">Y</span></li> 
       <li>There's lots of Original Research in the Infobox in each of the sections. These need citations since they're not stated in the prose.<img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/18px-X_mark.svg.png" decoding="async" width="18" height="21" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/27px-X_mark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/36px-X_mark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="525" data-file-height="600"> <b>Not done</b> 
        <ul>
         <li>National Public Broadcasting Archives says WVSS was named after Vocational Stout State, not Voice of Stout State.<img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/64/Purple_question_mark.svg/18px-Purple_question_mark.svg.png" decoding="async" width="18" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/64/Purple_question_mark.svg/27px-Purple_question_mark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/64/Purple_question_mark.svg/36px-Purple_question_mark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="450" data-file-height="450"> <b>Not sure</b></li>
        </ul></li> 
       <li>A lot of the prose mentioned in the lead in not mentioned at all in the history section. They need inclusion per <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Lead_section" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Lead section">Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Lead section</a>. I suggest rewriting this part to match what's in the history section while also including that this station is in Menomonie in the history section.<img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/18px-X_mark.svg.png" decoding="async" width="18" height="21" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/27px-X_mark.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/X_mark.svg/36px-X_mark.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="525" data-file-height="600"> <b>Not done</b></li>
      </ul> 
      <p>Overall, there's a lot of Original Research issues (some minor tweaks / some major issues), 1 minor word for word copy and a slight inaccuracy with the hook. As most of the criteria passes, I'm willing to keep this open so you can fix these issues. --<a href="/wiki/User:MrLinkinPark333" title="User:MrLinkinPark333">MrLinkinPark333</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:MrLinkinPark333" title="User talk:MrLinkinPark333">talk</a>) 20:51, 1 June 2021 (UTC) </p>

      <h4><span id="Robert_Jones_.28artilleryman.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Robert_Jones_(artilleryman)">Robert Jones (artilleryman)</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FRobert_Jones_%28artilleryman%29&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Robert_Jones_%28artilleryman%29&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 97px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Robert_Jones_sketch.jpg" class="image" title="Sketch of Robert Jones (c. 1772)"><img alt="Sketch of Robert Jones (c. 1772)" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Robert_Jones_sketch.jpg/97px-Robert_Jones_sketch.jpg" decoding="async" width="97" height="202" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Robert_Jones_sketch.jpg/146px-Robert_Jones_sketch.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Robert_Jones_sketch.jpg/194px-Robert_Jones_sketch.jpg 2x" data-file-width="378" data-file-height="787"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Sketch of Robert Jones (c. 1772)
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that in 1772, <b><a href="/wiki/Robert_Jones_(artilleryman)" title="Robert Jones (artilleryman)">Robert Jones</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> wrote the first book about <a href="/wiki/Figure_skating" title="Figure skating">figure skating</a>? <small>Source: Hines, James R. (2006). <i>Figure Skating: A History</i>. Urbana, Illinois: University of Chicago Press. ISBN 0-252-07286-3, p. 25</small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that in 1772, <b><a href="/wiki/Robert_Jones_(artilleryman)" title="Robert Jones (artilleryman)">Robert Jones</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> was convicted, sentenced to death, and exiled from England for <a href="/wiki/Sodomy" title="Sodomy">sodomy</a>? <small>Source: Rendell, Mike (2020). Sex and Sexuality in Georgian Britain. South Yorkshire, England: Pen and Sword History. ISBN 1526755637.</small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/American_Pre-Raphaelites" title="Template:Did you know nominations/American Pre-Raphaelites">Template:Did you know nominations/American Pre-Raphaelites</a></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <p><small>5x expanded by <a href="/wiki/User:Figureskatingfan" title="User:Figureskatingfan">Figureskatingfan</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Figureskatingfan" title="User talk:Figureskatingfan">talk</a>). Self-nominated at 18:11, 31 May 2021 (UTC).</small> </p>

      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2F1942_Eleftherias_Square_roundup&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li>

        </ul></li>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bucket_of_Blood_Street">Bucket of Blood Street</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FBucket_of_Blood_Street&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Bucket_of_Blood_Street&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 165px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Bucket_of_Blood_Street.jpg" class="image" title="Bucket of Blood Street"><img alt="Bucket of Blood Street" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Bucket_of_Blood_Street.jpg/165px-Bucket_of_Blood_Street.jpg" decoding="async" width="165" height="118" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Bucket_of_Blood_Street.jpg/248px-Bucket_of_Blood_Street.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Bucket_of_Blood_Street.jpg/330px-Bucket_of_Blood_Street.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1558" data-file-height="1118"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Bucket of Blood Street
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that <b><a href="/wiki/Bucket_of_Blood_Street" title="Bucket of Blood Street">Bucket of Blood Street</a></b> <i>(sign pictured)</i> and the Bucket of Blood Saloon are located in a town that had a reputation as “too tough for women and churches”? <small>Source: "While Holbrook is a friendly town today, in the mid-1880s the area was known as a place too tough for women and churches." <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://kjzz.org/content/1180891/qaz-how-did-holbrooks-bucket-blood-street-get-its-name">[34]</a>, "Surrounded by the Navajo, Hopi, Zuni and Apache tribes, the town was neither inviting nor safe for families and was dubbed the “town too tough for women and churches.” <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://tribunenewsnow.com/holbrooks-history-details-the-true-story-of-the-wild-west/">[35]</a>, "This led to the town earning a reputation as one “too tough for women and churches.” <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.onlyinyourstate.com/arizona/az-bucket-of-blood/">[36]</a></small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that the Bucket of Blood Saloon on <b><a href="/wiki/Bucket_of_Blood_Street" title="Bucket of Blood Street">Bucket of Blood Street</a></b> <i>(sign pictured)</i> are in a town with a reputation as "too tough for women and churches"? <small>Source: Same sources as in above hook, but slightly different wording.</small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul>

       <dd>

      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FEmbassy_of_the_United_States%2C_Phnom_Penh&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li>

      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that Cambodian leader <a href="/wiki/Hun_Sen" title="Hun Sen">Hun Sen</a> released four imprisoned dissidents as a "gift" to the United States upon the commencement of its <b><a href="/wiki/Embassy_of_the_United_States,_Phnom_Penh" title="Embassy of the United States, Phnom Penh">new embassy in Phnom Penh</a></b>? <small>Source: " The Cambodian government on Tuesday released four imprisoned government critics... Om Yentieng, an adviser to Hun Sen, quoted the prime minister as saying he had made the bail request as "a gift for Mr. Christopher Hill on the inauguration of the new U.S. Embassy." <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/archive/politics/2006/01/18/cambodia-releases-4-political-dissidents/7e511aa6-ce2d-4f07-bbad-aee70ae4532c/">1</a></small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that <a href="/wiki/UNESCO" title="UNESCO">UNESCO</a> objected to a possible site for the <b><a href="/wiki/Embassy_of_the_United_States,_Phnom_Penh" title="Embassy of the United States, Phnom Penh">new US embassy complex in Phnom Penh</a></b>, but it was the one chosen anyway? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.phnompenhpost.com/national/sparks-fly-over-us-wat-phnom-embassy-plan">2</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://english.cambodiadaily.com/news/us-embassy-unveils-new-site-35169/">3</a></small></li> 
         <li><b>ALT2</b>:... that the current complex of the <b><a href="/wiki/Embassy_of_the_United_States,_Phnom_Penh" title="Embassy of the United States, Phnom Penh">US embassy in Phnom Penh</a></b> was a "flagship project"? <small>Source: "The new embassy will be “a flagship project for a new generation” of US embassies around the world,” Williams (referring to "Charles Williams, the director and chief operating officer of the US State Department’s Overseas Building Operations") said." <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://english.cambodiadaily.com/news/us-embassy-unveils-new-site-35169/">4</a></small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul>

       <dd>

      <ul>
       <li>... that Swedish writer <b><a href="/wiki/Hedda_Anderson" title="Hedda Anderson">Hedda Anderson</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> began her literary career at the age of 58, following her husband's death in 1888? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.skbl.se/sv/artikel/HedvigHeddaElisabetAnderson">"In 1888 Johan Elis Anderson died. Two years later, the then 58-year-old Hedda Anderson moved to Stockholm. In connection with this move, she began her writing career."</a></small></li>
      </ul>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Chipozi_zhuan">Chipozi zhuan</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FChipozi_zhuan&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li>

      <ul>
       <li>... that in a Chinese erotic novella titled <i><b><a href="/wiki/Chipozi_zhuan" title="Chipozi zhuan">Chipozi zhuan</a></b></i>, a woman has sex with her cousin, her brothers-in-law, her father-in-law, and two Buddhist monks?</li>
      </ul>

       <dd>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bush_Tower">Bush Tower</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FBush_Tower&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Bush_Tower&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 121px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Bush_Tower-04.jpg" class="image" title="Bush Tower"><img alt="Bush Tower" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Bush_Tower-04.jpg/121px-Bush_Tower-04.jpg" decoding="async" width="121" height="161" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Bush_Tower-04.jpg/182px-Bush_Tower-04.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/db/Bush_Tower-04.jpg/242px-Bush_Tower-04.jpg 2x" data-file-width="768" data-file-height="1024"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Bush Tower
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that New York City's <b><a href="/wiki/Bush_Tower" title="Bush Tower">Bush Tower</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i>, whose volume was compared to an arrow, was intended as a model for skyscrapers in the middle of city blocks? <small>Source: (1) Kimball, Fiske (1928). American architecture. Indianapolis; New York: The Bobbs-Merrill Company. p. 205. (2) Corbett, Harvey Wiley (1930). "The Bush Building". In Hoak, Edward Warren; Church, Willis Humphry (eds.). Masterpieces of American Architecture. Dover Architecture. Dover Publications. p. 195.</small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that the <b><a href="/wiki/Bush_Tower" title="Bush Tower">Bush Tower</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i>, near New York City's Times Square, was an attempt at a trade center before the <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Center_(1973%E2%80%932001)" title="World Trade Center (1973–2001)">World Trade Center</a> itself? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2015/04/30/nyregion/restoring-a-bit-of-old-english-flair-to-a-skyscraper-on-42nd-street.html">Dunlap, David W. (April 29, 2015). "A Bit of Gothic Flair Returns to a Tower on 42nd Street". The New York Times.</a></small></li> 
         <li><b>ALT2</b>:... that the <b><a href="/wiki/Bush_Tower" title="Bush Tower">Bush Tower</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i>, once the tallest in Midtown Manhattan, contained manufacturers' showrooms in a concept likened to a museum? <small>Source: Stern, Robert A. M.; Gilmartin, Patrick; Mellins, Thomas (1987). New York 1930: Architecture and Urbanism Between the Two World Wars. New York: Rizzoli. p. 546.</small></li> 
         <li><b>ALT3</b>:... that the <b><a href="/wiki/Bush_Tower" title="Bush Tower">Bush Tower</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i>, originally a manufacturers' showroom and Midtown Manhattan's tallest building, later contained a porn theater and was considered for demolition? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nytimes.com/1985/05/22/business/about-real-estate-renewal-of-west-42d-st-tower-is-nearly-completed.html">Depalma, Anthony (May 22, 1985). "About Real Estate; Renewal of West 42d St. Tower Is Nearly Completed". The New York Times.</a></small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Margit_Abenius" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Margit Abenius">Margit Abenius</a></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: I can propose more hooks if these are not satisfactory</li>
        </ul>

        </dl>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <div style="clear:both;"></div> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Margit_Abenius">Margit Abenius</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FMargit_Abenius&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Margit_Abenius&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 108px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Margit_Abenius_(1920-talet).jpg" class="image" title="Margit Abenius"><img alt="Margit Abenius" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Margit_Abenius_%281920-talet%29.jpg/108px-Margit_Abenius_%281920-talet%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="108" height="183" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/Margit_Abenius_%281920-talet%29.jpg/162px-Margit_Abenius_%281920-talet%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/8d/Margit_Abenius_%281920-talet%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="210" data-file-height="355"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Margit Abenius
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that the biography of <a href="/wiki/Karin_Boye" title="Karin Boye">Karin Boye</a>, written by Swedish literary critic <b><a href="/wiki/Margit_Abenius" title="Margit Abenius">Margit Abenius</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i>, was criticised for the conservative analysis of Boye's homosexuality? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.skbl.se/sv/artikel/MargitAbenius">[37]</a></small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that Swedish literary critic <b><a href="/wiki/Margit_Abenius" title="Margit Abenius">Margit Abenius</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i>, who is best known for her biography of <a href="/wiki/Karin_Boye" title="Karin Boye">Karin Boye</a>, is one of the leading voices of the Swedish literary canon in the 20th century? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.co.in/books?id=8JrxRm0CDvEC">[38]</a></small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Line_3_oil_spill" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Line 3 oil spill">Line 3 oil spill</a></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: The first source is in Swedish.</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl>

        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Daisy advertisement
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that although the <a href="/wiki/Daisy_(advertisement)" title="Daisy (advertisement)">Daisy ad</a> <i>(pictured)</i> was aired only once, it is considered to be one of the most important factors for victory in <b><a href="/wiki/Lyndon_B._Johnson_1964_presidential_campaign" title="Lyndon B. Johnson 1964 presidential campaign">Lyndon B. Johnson's 1964 presidential campaign</a></b>? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://blog.apaonline.org/2020/12/30/the-daisy-ad-and-an-appeal-to-fear/">The Daisy Ad and an Appeal to Fear</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.smithsonianmag.com/history/how-daisy-ad-changed-everything-about-political-advertising-180958741/">How the “Daisy” Ad Changed Everything About Political Advertising: <i>Smithsoian</i> magazine</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://blogs.loc.gov/now-see-hear/2016/09/daisy-the-most-effective-political-commercial-ever/">Library of Congress</a></small></li>
      </ul>

         <li><a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_question.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol question.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/16px-Symbol_question.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/24px-Symbol_question.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/32px-Symbol_question.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> Article is a new spin-off, that is clearly notable. Hook is cited to the <i>Smithsoian</i>. I admit I was more interested in the Daisy advertisement than the campaign article, but that means the hook is certainly attention grabbing. There are a few formatting errors on the talk page, and the spin-off needs to note any copied content properly for attribution purposes. Earwig's bot reports close paraphrasing of the "Because tonight the contest is the same..." speech, which is a direct quotation, but may be worth trimming. I can't remember if US Federal Government campaign speeches are public domain or not, can you advise? <a href="/wiki/User:Ritchie333" title="User:Ritchie333"><b style="color:#7F007F">Ritchie333</b></a> <a href="/wiki/User_talk:Ritchie333" title="User talk:Ritchie333"><sup style="color:#7F007F">(talk)</sup></a> <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Ritchie333" title="Special:Contributions/Ritchie333"><sup style="color:#7F007F">(cont)</sup></a> 20:35, 3 June 2021 (UTC)</li>
        </ul>

      <h3><span id="Articles_created.2Fexpanded_on_June_4"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Articles_created/expanded_on_June_4">Articles created/expanded on June 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know/Approved&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Articles created/expanded on June 4">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span id="William_Gregson_.28slave_trader.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="William_Gregson_(slave_trader)">William Gregson (slave trader)</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FWilliam_Gregson_%28slave_trader%29&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=William_Gregson_%28slave_trader%29&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 148px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Zong_massacre.jpg" class="image" title="Zong massacre"><img alt="Zong massacre" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Zong_massacre.jpg/148px-Zong_massacre.jpg" decoding="async" width="148" height="133" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cd/Zong_massacre.jpg/222px-Zong_massacre.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/cd/Zong_massacre.jpg 2x" data-file-width="250" data-file-height="225"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         <i>Zong</i> massacre
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that in a court case <b><a href="/wiki/William_Gregson_(slave_trader)" title="William Gregson (slave trader)">William Gregson</a></b> was awarded £30 for every slave that his crew had murdered in the <a href="/wiki/Zong_massacre" title="Zong massacre"><i>Zong</i> massacre</a>?</li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><small><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.co.uk/books?id=kIp9er6RDyYC&amp;redir_esc=y">this book</a> says on page 102 "What stunned people about the Zong in March 1783 was not simply the murderous brutality of events on that ship, but the incredible legal saga played out in London – and the implications of that legal debate. An English jury, sitting under the watchful gaze of the Lord Chief Justice, Lord Mansfield, ‘rendered a verdict wholly favourable to the owners of the Zong for the loss of 130-plus slaves at £30"</small></li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <p><small>Created by <a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Desertarun&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Desertarun (page does not exist)">Desertarun</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Desertarun" title="User talk:Desertarun">talk</a>). Self-nominated at 07:30, 5 June 2021 (UTC).</small> </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_question.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol question.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/16px-Symbol_question.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/24px-Symbol_question.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/32px-Symbol_question.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> Date, length, writing all check out, no apparent copyvio. I did some light copy-editing on the article. The hook certainly caught my attention. <s>My only concern about putting this on the front page is the citations to a "Visit Lancaster" article which is just an unattributed MS Word pdf and seems a bit dubious as a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:RS" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:RS">reliable source</a>. Is there any chance you could track those down from a better source? The article does have a bibliography so it shouldn't be too hard to follow up.</s> —<a href="/wiki/User:Nizolan" title="User:Nizolan">Nizolan</a> <sup>(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Nizolan" title="User talk:Nizolan">talk</a> · <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Nizolan" title="Special:Contributions/Nizolan">c.</a>)</sup> 23:51, 5 June 2021 (UTC)</li> 
         <li><a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_confirmed.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol confirmed.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Symbol_confirmed.svg/16px-Symbol_confirmed.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Symbol_confirmed.svg/24px-Symbol_confirmed.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Symbol_confirmed.svg/32px-Symbol_confirmed.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> As luck would have it I discovered the published version of the article <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://visitlancaster.org.uk/wordpress/wp-content/uploads/2021/02/Biographies-of-individuals-involved-in-the-Zong-massacre.pdf">here</a>, which now looks reputable. I've swapped that in and done some more minor editing on the article. Happy for this go ahead now. —<a href="/wiki/User:Nizolan" title="User:Nizolan">Nizolan</a> <sup>(<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Nizolan" title="User talk:Nizolan">talk</a> · <a href="/wiki/Special:Contributions/Nizolan" title="Special:Contributions/Nizolan">c.</a>)</sup> 02:39, 6 June 2021 (UTC)</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Song_of_Iowa">The Song of Iowa</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FThe_Song_of_Iowa&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=The_Song_of_Iowa&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: px;"> 
        <div class="mediaContainer" style="width:220px">
         <audio id="mwe_player_2" controls="" preload="none" style="width:220px" class="kskin" data-durationhint="44.680997732426" data-startoffset="0" data-mwtitle="&quot;O_Tannenbaum&quot;.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons">

      <ul>
       <li>... that Major Byers wrote "<b><a href="/wiki/The_Song_of_Iowa" title="The Song of Iowa">The Song of Iowa</a></b>" after being inspired by hearing Confederate soldiers playing "<a href="/wiki/Maryland,_My_Maryland" title="Maryland, My Maryland">Maryland, My Maryland</a>" outside his prison cell and used the same tune <i>(included)</i>? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.newspapers.com/image/3160200/?terms=%22song%20of%20iowa%22&amp;match=1">Newspapers.com</a></small></li>
      </ul>

         <li><i>Comment</i>: Expansion made excluding the lyrics</li>
        </ul>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Special_occasion_holding_area">Special occasion holding area</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know/Approved&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Special occasion holding area">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Do <b>not</b> nominate articles in this section—nominate all articles in the <a href="/wiki/Template_talk:Did_you_know#Nominations" title="Template talk:Did you know">nominations</a> section on the regular nominations page, under the date on which the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:DYKTN#article" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:DYKTN">article</a> was created or moved to mainspace, or the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:DYKTN#expansion" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:DYKTN">expansion</a> began, or it was listed as a <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:GA" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:GA">Good Article</a>; be sure to indicate in the nomination any request for a specially timed appearance on the main page.
      </div> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       Note: Articles intended to be held for special occasion dates should be nominated within seven days of creation, start of expansion, or promotion to Good Article status. The nomination should be made between at least one week prior to the occasion date, to allow time for reviews and promotions through the prep and queue sets, but not more than six weeks in advance. The proposed occasion must be deemed sufficiently special by reviewers. The timeline limitations, including the six week maximum, may be waived by consensus, if a request is made at <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia_talk:DYK" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia talk:DYK">WT:DYK</a>, but requests are not always successful. Discussion clarifying the hold criteria can be found here: <a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia_talk:Did_you_know/Archive_161#Revision_3">[39]</a>; discussion setting the six week limit can be found here: <a class="external autonumber" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia_talk:Did_you_know/Archive_65#Rhacophorus_vampyrus">[40]</a>.
      </div> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       April Fools' Day hooks are exempted from the timeline limit; see <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:April_Fool%27s_Main_Page/Did_You_Know" title="Wikipedia:April Fool's Main Page/Did You Know">Wikipedia:April Fool's Main Page/Did You Know</a></b>.
      </div> 
      <h3><span id="June_14_.28anniversary.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="June_14_(anniversary)">June 14 (anniversary)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know/Approved&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: June 14 (anniversary)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="White_flags_over_Port_Stanley">White flags over Port Stanley</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FWhite_flags_over_Port_Stanley&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=White_flags_over_Port_Stanley&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 127px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Prime_Minister_Margaret_Thatcher.jpg" class="image" title="Thatcher in June 1982"><img alt="Thatcher in June 1982" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Prime_Minister_Margaret_Thatcher.jpg/127px-Prime_Minister_Margaret_Thatcher.jpg" decoding="async" width="127" height="154" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Prime_Minister_Margaret_Thatcher.jpg/191px-Prime_Minister_Margaret_Thatcher.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Prime_Minister_Margaret_Thatcher.jpg/254px-Prime_Minister_Margaret_Thatcher.jpg 2x" data-file-width="481" data-file-height="585"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Thatcher in June 1982
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that although <a href="/wiki/Margaret_Thatcher" title="Margaret Thatcher">Margaret Thatcher</a> <i>(pictured)</i> announced to the House of Commons on 14 June 1982 that Argentine troops were "<b><a href="/wiki/White_flags_over_Port_Stanley" title="White flags over Port Stanley">flying white flags over Port Stanley</a></b>", it was probably just laundry on a washing line? <small>"20 years after the end of the Falklands War the myth of 'white flags flying over Stanley' on the morning of 14 June 1982, has finally been exploded ... So what was the mysterious white object which was sighted by 'A' Company? Major Dawson readily agrees that 'It was probably someone washing hanging on a clothes line'" from: 
         <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r999302996"><cite id="CITEREFWatts2002" class="citation news cs1">Watts, Patrick (12 November 2002). <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://en.mercopress.com/2002/11/12/white-flags-over-stanley">"White flags over Stanley"</a>. <i>MercoPress</i><span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">13 May</span> 2021</span>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=MercoPress&amp;rft.atitle=White+flags+over+Stanley&amp;rft.date=2002-11-12&amp;rft.aulast=Watts&amp;rft.aufirst=Patrick&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fen.mercopress.com%2F2002%2F11%2F12%2Fwhite-flags-over-stanley&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ATemplate+talk%3ADid+you+know%2FApproved" class="Z3988"></span></small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that on 14 June 1982 <a href="/wiki/Margaret_Thatcher" title="Margaret Thatcher">Margaret Thatcher</a> <i>(pictured)</i> delayed announcing that Argentine troops were "<b><a href="/wiki/White_flags_over_Port_Stanley" title="White flags over Port Stanley">flying white flags over Port Stanley</a></b>" so that it could be covered live on the <i><a href="/wiki/ITV_News_at_Ten" title="ITV News at Ten">ITN News at Ten</a></i>? <small>"On 14 June 1982, after the fall of Port Stanley, Downing Street imposed a complete news blackout on reporters in the Falkands which lasted nine hours. The prime minister was delaying her announcement to the Commons that the Argentine forces were now flying white flags so that ITN's News at Ten would broadcast it live." from: 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r999302996"><cite id="CITEREFRobinson2013" class="citation book cs1">Robinson, Nick (2013). <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.google.co.uk/books/edition/Live_from_Downing_Street/cHMgAgAAQBAJ"><i>Live from Downing Street: The Inside Story of Politics, Power and the Media</i></a>. London: Bantam Press. p.&nbsp;231. <a href="/wiki/ISBN_(identifier)" class="mw-redirect" title="ISBN (identifier)">ISBN</a>&nbsp;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-85750-000-7" title="Special:BookSources/978-0-85750-000-7"><bdi>978-0-85750-000-7</bdi></a>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=Live+from+Downing+Street%3A+The+Inside+Story+of+Politics%2C+Power+and+the+Media&amp;rft.place=London&amp;rft.pages=231&amp;rft.pub=Bantam+Press&amp;rft.date=2013&amp;rft.isbn=978-0-85750-000-7&amp;rft.aulast=Robinson&amp;rft.aufirst=Nick&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.google.co.uk%2Fbooks%2Fedition%2FLive_from_Downing_Street%2FcHMgAgAAQBAJ&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ATemplate+talk%3ADid+you+know%2FApproved" class="Z3988"></span></small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/KFBX" title="Template:Did you know nominations/KFBX">Template:Did you know nominations/KFBX</a></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: Date request for anniversary on 14 June</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>

      <h3><span id="July_TBC_.28Stanley_Cup_final.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="July_TBC_(Stanley_Cup_final)">July TBC (Stanley Cup final)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know/Approved&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: July TBC (Stanley Cup final)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gilles_Lupien">Gilles Lupien</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FGilles_Lupien&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Gilles_Lupien&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that <b><a href="/wiki/Gilles_Lupien" title="Gilles Lupien">Gilles Lupien</a></b> used the <a href="/wiki/Canadian_dollar" title="Canadian dollar">C$</a>75,000 <a href="/wiki/Signing_bonus" title="Signing bonus">signing bonus</a> from his first <a href="/wiki/Montreal_Canadiens" title="Montreal Canadiens">Montreal Canadiens</a> contract to buy shares in a <a href="/wiki/Lumber" title="Lumber">lumber</a> company, enabling him to obtain quality lumber to construct his first home? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://montrealgazette.com/sports/hockey/nhl/hockey-inside-out/former-canadiens-defenceman-gilles-lupien-dies-from-cancer-at-age-67"><i>Montreal Gazette</i></a></small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that <b><a href="/wiki/Gilles_Lupien" title="Gilles Lupien">Gilles Lupien</a></b> purchased a <a href="/wiki/Humpty_Dumpty_Snack_Foods" title="Humpty Dumpty Snack Foods">Humpty Dumpty Snack Foods</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Boston_Pizza" title="Boston Pizza">Boston Pizza</a> franchise after his <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_League" title="National Hockey League">National Hockey League</a> career? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://montrealgazette.com/sports/hockey/nhl/hockey-inside-out/former-canadiens-defenceman-gilles-lupien-dies-from-cancer-at-age-67"><i>Montreal Gazette</i></a></small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Pelican_Portrait" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Pelican Portrait">Pelican Portrait</a></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: Please <b>save for the start of the Stanley Cup Finals</b>, date TBD (July 15 being the tentative <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nhl.com/hurricanes/news/key-dates-2020-21-nhl-season/c-319844126">last possible date</a>). Eligible per <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Did_you_know#Eligibility_criteria" title="Wikipedia:Did you know">Rule 1d</a>, because it only appeared in the "Recent Deaths" section of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:In_the_news" title="Wikipedia:In the news">ITN</a> and not as a bold link.</li>
        </ul>

      <h3><span id="July_1_.28Canada_Day.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="July_1_(Canada_Day)">July 1 (Canada Day)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know/Approved&amp;action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: July 1 (Canada Day)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="John_Mercer_Johnson">John Mercer Johnson</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FJohn_Mercer_Johnson&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=John_Mercer_Johnson&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 110px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:John_Mercer_Johnson.jpeg" class="image" title="John Mercer Johnson"><img alt="John Mercer Johnson" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b3/John_Mercer_Johnson.jpeg/110px-John_Mercer_Johnson.jpeg" decoding="async" width="110" height="178" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b3/John_Mercer_Johnson.jpeg 1.5x" data-file-width="142" data-file-height="230"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         John Mercer Johnson
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that <b><a href="/wiki/John_Mercer_Johnson" title="John Mercer Johnson">John Mercer Johnson</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i>, a <a href="/wiki/Fathers_of_Confederation" title="Fathers of Confederation">Father of Canadian Confederation</a>, entertained the public and members of the <a href="/wiki/London_Conference_of_1866" title="London Conference of 1866">London Conference of 1866</a> with poetry readings and ice skating performances? <small>Source: "he is referred to as one of the Fathers of Confederation." <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.gnb.ca/legis/speakers/bios/johnson-john-e.asp">[41]</a> "One of the great stories about Johnson was at the London Conference. While there he dazzled the public and the members with his poetry presentations and his dazzling ice skating performances."</small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that <b><a href="/wiki/John_Mercer_Johnson" title="John Mercer Johnson">John Mercer Johnson</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> was one of eleven <a href="/wiki/Fathers_of_Confederation" title="Fathers of Confederation">Fathers of Canadian Confederation</a> to attend all three conferences that led to the creation of Canada? <small>Source: "Pourtant, seulement onze individus sont présents à chacune de ces trois conférences initiales. Ce sont...John Mercer Johnson et Samuel L. Tully du Nouveau-Brunswick" <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.erudit.org/fr/revues/cd/2014-n119-cd01541/72695ac/">[42]</a></small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Museum_of_Literature_Ireland" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Museum of Literature Ireland">Template:Did you know nominations/Museum of Literature Ireland</a></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: Please run on July 1, Canada Day.</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Canadian_Idiot">Canadian Idiot</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FCanadian_Idiot&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Canadian_Idiot&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that the song "<b><a href="/wiki/Canadian_Idiot" title="Canadian Idiot">Canadian Idiot</a></b>" satirizes American <a href="/wiki/Xenophobia" title="Xenophobia">xenophobia</a>? <small>Source: "Yankovic's insult song is actually a send-up of the rude American more than the Canadian." ... "'Canadian Idiot' is fundamentally about the way we demonize people who are not like us," Lily Hirsch and Nathan Rabin, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=r8vADwAAQBAJ"><i>Weird Al: Seriously</i></a> p. 109. The latter part is online at <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nathanrabin.com/happy-place/2018/6/4/day-one-hundred-and-thirty-two-canadian-idiot-from-straight-outta-lynwood">Nathan Rabin's Happy Place blog.</a></small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that <a href="/wiki/%22Weird_Al%22_Yankovic" title="&quot;Weird Al&quot; Yankovic">"Weird Al" Yankovic</a> told his audience "thanks for not killing us" after his first performance of "<b><a href="/wiki/Canadian_Idiot" title="Canadian Idiot">Canadian Idiot</a></b>" in the title country? <span style="font-size:85%;">Source: <i>Winnipeg Sun</i> 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r999302996"><a href="/wiki/ProQuest_(identifier)" class="mw-redirect" title="ProQuest (identifier)">ProQuest</a>&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://search.proquest.com/docview/2171042160">2171042160</a></span></li> 
         <li><b>ALT2</b>:... that the <i><a href="/wiki/Toronto_Star" title="Toronto Star">Toronto Star</a></i> put "<b><a href="/wiki/Canadian_Idiot" title="Canadian Idiot">Canadian Idiot</a></b>" on its 'naughty list' for encouraging the mocking of Canada? <span style="font-size:85%;">Source: <i>Toronto Star</i> 
           <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r999302996"><a href="/wiki/ProQuest_(identifier)" class="mw-redirect" title="ProQuest (identifier)">ProQuest</a>&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://search.proquest.com/docview/439117098">439117098</a> </span></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Thorne_miniature_rooms" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Thorne miniature rooms">Template:Did you know nominations/Thorne miniature rooms</a></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: This year is the 15th anniversary of the song's release. Would appreciate if this could run on 1 July (<a href="/wiki/Canada_Day" title="Canada Day">Canada Day</a>) or otherwise around 1–4 July.</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Walter_Bean_Grand_River_Trail">Walter Bean Grand River Trail</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FWalter_Bean_Grand_River_Trail&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Walter_Bean_Grand_River_Trail&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that the <b><a href="/wiki/Walter_Bean_Grand_River_Trail" title="Walter Bean Grand River Trail">Walter Bean Grand River Trail</a></b> was named after Walter Bean, who created the idea of a continuous trail through the <a href="/wiki/Regional_Municipality_of_Waterloo" title="Regional Municipality of Waterloo">Waterloo Region</a>? 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that a southern section of the <b><a href="/wiki/Walter_Bean_Grand_River_Trail" title="Walter Bean Grand River Trail">Walter Bean Grand River Trail</a></b> in <a href="/wiki/Regional_Municipality_of_Waterloo" title="Regional Municipality of Waterloo">Waterloo Region</a>, is part of the <a href="/wiki/Trans_Canada_Trail" title="Trans Canada Trail">Trans Canada Trail</a>?</li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li class="mw-empty-elt"></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: Source for hook 1: <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.kitchener.ca/en/parks-and-trails/walter-bean-grand-river-trail.aspx">[43]</a>; source for hook 2: <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.worldcat.org/title/grand-river-ontario-a-decade-in-ths-canadian-heritage-rivers-system-a-review-of-the-grand-strategy/oclc/56923100">[44]</a>.</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl>

That would indeed be interesting, but the article needs to state that. <a href="/wiki/User:Wasted_Time_R" title="User:Wasted Time R">Wasted Time R</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Wasted_Time_R" title="User talk:Wasted Time R">talk</a>) 23:34, 27 May 2021 (UTC)

                  <span class="template-ping">@<a href="/wiki/User:Wasted_Time_R" title="User:Wasted Time R">Wasted Time R</a>:</span> It's a bit odd, the Trans Canada Trail isn't linear and takes 2 routes through Southern Ontario. The Walter Bean Trail actually makes up a part of the TCT in Cambridge (I actually didn't realize because the source didn't mention it, but the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://thegreattrail.ca/explore-the-map/">official map</a> does). But no, the southernmost point of the Trans Canada Trail is not intersected by Walter Bean. The southernmost point of Walter Bean connects (and is part of) the TCT. I've clarified ALT1 and the article, thanks! It both "connects" and "is part of" the TCT, so while the old hook was still correct, what I changed it to is more accurate (although somehow more dull imo).

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Flag_of_Nova_Scotia">Flag of Nova Scotia</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FFlag_of_Nova_Scotia&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Flag_of_Nova_Scotia&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 200px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_Nova_Scotia.svg" class="image" title="Flag of Nova Scotia"><img alt="Flag of Nova Scotia" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Flag_of_Nova_Scotia.svg/198px-Flag_of_Nova_Scotia.svg.png" decoding="async" width="198" height="99" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Flag_of_Nova_Scotia.svg/297px-Flag_of_Nova_Scotia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Flag_of_Nova_Scotia.svg/396px-Flag_of_Nova_Scotia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Flag of Nova Scotia
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that the <b><a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Nova_Scotia" title="Flag of Nova Scotia">flag of Nova Scotia</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> was officially recognized in 2013, even though its first documented usage was in June 1858? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://nslegislature.ca/legc/bills/61st_5th/3rd_read/b082.htm"><i>Provincial Flag Act</i></a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.cbc.ca/news/canada/nova-scotia/nova-scotia-s-provincial-flag-confirmed-155-years-later-1.1335703">CBC News</a></small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that the <b><a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Nova_Scotia" title="Flag of Nova Scotia">flag of Nova Scotia</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> was the first flag in the overseas <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_realm" title="Commonwealth realm">Commonwealth</a> to be approved by royal charter? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.canada.ca/en/canadian-heritage/services/provincial-territorial-symbols-canada/nova-scotia.html#a5">Department of Canadian Heritage</a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://nslegislature.ca/about/photo-galleries/symbols/flag-nova-scotia">Nova Scotia House of Assembly</a></small></li> 
         <li><b>ALT2</b>:... that the <b><a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Nova_Scotia" title="Flag of Nova Scotia">flag of Nova Scotia</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> is the oldest provincial flag in Canada? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=KuikAwAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PA28"><i>Our Flag: The Story of Canada's Maple Leaf</i></a></small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Fran%C3%A7ois_Henri_Mouton" title="Template:Did you know nominations/François Henri Mouton">François Henri Mouton</a></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: Please <b>save for July 1</b>, <a href="/wiki/Canada_Day" title="Canada Day">Canada Day</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(exactly 4 weeks and 5 days from now)</span>.</li>
        </ul>

      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Murray_Dowey">Murray Dowey</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FMurray_Dowey&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Murray_Dowey&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that <b><a href="/wiki/Murray_Dowey" title="Murray Dowey">Murray Dowey</a></b> was a clerk and typist for the <a href="/wiki/Toronto_Transit_Commission" title="Toronto Transit Commission">Toronto Transit Commission</a> before being the <a href="/wiki/Goaltender" title="Goaltender">goaltender</a> for Canada's gold medal-winning hockey team at the <a href="/wiki/1948_Winter_Olympics" title="1948 Winter Olympics">1948 Winter Olympics</a>? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://ottawacitizen.com/sports/olympics/70-years-ago-murray-dowey-backstopped-another-crew-of-canadian-amateurs-to-winter-olympic-hockey-glory"><i>Ottawa Citizen</i></a></small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that <b><a href="/wiki/Murray_Dowey" title="Murray Dowey">Murray Dowey</a></b><span class="nowrap">'s</span> five <a href="/wiki/Shutout#Ice_hockey" title="Shutout">shutouts</a> and 0.62 <a href="/wiki/Goals_against_average" title="Goals against average">goals against average</a> at the <a href="/wiki/1948_Winter_Olympics" title="1948 Winter Olympics">1948 Winter Olympics</a> remain Olympic records to this day? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.iihf.com/en/events/2021/wm/news/26008/murray_dowey_1925-2021">International Ice Hockey Federation</a></small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Ekkehard_von_Kuenssberg" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Ekkehard von Kuenssberg">Ekkehard von Kuenssberg</a></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: Please <b>save for July 1</b>, <a href="/wiki/Canada_Day" title="Canada Day">Canada Day</a> <span style="font-size:85%;">(exactly 4 weeks and 4 days from now)</span>. Eligible per <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Did_you_know#Eligibility_criteria" title="Wikipedia:Did you know">Rule 1d</a>, because it is only scheduled to appear in the "Recent Deaths" section of <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:In_the_news" title="Wikipedia:In the news">ITN</a> and not as a bold link.</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl>

Although ALT1 is not stated in the article, it does state that the record holds at the time of his death, which was May 29, 2021. One of the sources mentions that the record holds today, and since a winter Olympics is not scheduled until 2022, the record will hold for at least a few months. I imagine that the article doesn't say "current record holder" because of <a href="/wiki/MOS:DATED" class="mw-redirect" title="MOS:DATED">MOS:DATED</a> so I'm willing to <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:IAR" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:IAR">WP:IAR</a> and approve ALT1. <a href="/wiki/User:Z1720" title="User:Z1720">Z1720</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Z1720" title="User talk:Z1720">talk</a>) 16:16, 30 May 2021 (UTC) </p>

      <h3><span id="July_4_.28US_Independence_Day.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="July_4_(US_Independence_Day)">July 4 (US Independence Day)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know/Approved&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: July 4 (US Independence Day)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Rhodesian_Independence_Bell">Rhodesian Independence Bell</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FRhodesian_Independence_Bell&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Rhodesian_Independence_Bell&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that the <b><a href="/wiki/Rhodesian_Independence_Bell" title="Rhodesian Independence Bell">Rhodesian Independence Bell</a></b>, a replica of the American <a href="/wiki/Liberty_Bell" title="Liberty Bell">Liberty Bell</a>, was inscribed "I toll for justice, civilization and Christianity"? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nytimes.com/1976/11/12/archives/rhodesians-celebrate-11th-anniversary-of-breakaway-anniversary-of.html">New York Times</a></small></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Lord_Grizzly" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Lord Grizzly">Lord Grizzly</a></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: For 4th July (<s>Treason Day</s> American Independence Day)</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl>

       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_confirmed.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol confirmed.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Symbol_confirmed.svg/16px-Symbol_confirmed.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Symbol_confirmed.svg/24px-Symbol_confirmed.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Symbol_confirmed.svg/32px-Symbol_confirmed.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> New enough, long enough, and within policy (neutral, no copvyio, inline citations). Nominator's QPQ confirmed. Hook is interesting, short enough, backed up by an inline citation in the article, and neutral. Let me make one suggestion: I think the two instances of "was" are a little otiose, I'll make a slight change to the hook to avoid them. I believe this change will be so minimal that it won't require the attention of another reviewer. Good to go. <a href="/wiki/User:Modussiccandi" title="User:Modussiccandi">Modussiccandi</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Modussiccandi" title="User talk:Modussiccandi">talk</a>) 14:36, 27 May 2021 (UTC)</li>
