      <h3><span id="July_5_.28Constitution_Day.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="July_5_(Constitution_Day)">July 5 (Constitution Day)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Template_talk:Did_you_know/Approved&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: July 5 (Constitution Day)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3> 
      <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands">Flag of the Cayman Islands</span></h4> 
      <div class="plainlinks hlist"> 
       <ul>
        <li>( <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Template%3ADid_you_know_nominations%2FFlag_of_the_Cayman_Islands&amp;action=edit">Review or comment</a></li> 
        <li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands&amp;action=history">Article history</a> )</li>
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <div class="dyk-img" style="float: right; margin-left: 0.5em;"> 
       <div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 198px;"> <a href="/wiki/File:Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg" class="image" title="Flag of the Cayman Islands"><img alt="Flag of the Cayman Islands" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg/198px-Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="198" height="99" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg/297px-Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0f/Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg/396px-Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600"></a>
        <div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word;">
         Flag of the Cayman Islands
        </div>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <ul>
       <li>... that the turtle on the <b><a href="/wiki/Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands" title="Flag of the Cayman Islands">flag of the Cayman Islands</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> alludes to the original Spanish name for the islands, <i>Las Tortugas</i><span style="padding-left:0.15em;">?</span> <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.britannica.com/topic/flag-of-Cayman-Islands"><i>Encyclopedia Britannica</i></a></small> 
        <ul>
         <li><b>ALT1</b>:... that the three green stars on the <b><a href="/wiki/Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands" title="Flag of the Cayman Islands">flag of the Cayman Islands</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> represent the territory's three islands of <a href="/wiki/Grand_Cayman" title="Grand Cayman">Grand Cayman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Little_Cayman" title="Little Cayman">Little Cayman</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Cayman_Brac" title="Cayman Brac">Cayman Brac</a>? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.britannica.com/topic/flag-of-Cayman-Islands"><i>Encyclopedia Britannica</i></a>; <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.cia.gov/the-world-factbook/countries/cayman-islands/flag">CIA World Factbook</a></small></li> 
         <li><b>ALT2</b>:... that the pineapple on the <b><a href="/wiki/Flag_of_the_Cayman_Islands" title="Flag of the Cayman Islands">flag of the Cayman Islands</a></b> <i>(pictured)</i> alludes to the territory's historic connection with Jamaica, whose <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_Jamaica" title="Coat of arms of Jamaica">coat of arms</a> features five pineapples? <small>Source: <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.britannica.com/topic/flag-of-Cayman-Islands"><i>Encyclopedia Britannica</i></a></small></li>
        </ul></li>
      </ul> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><i>Reviewed</i>: <a href="/wiki/Template:Did_you_know_nominations/Joe_DiMaggio%27s_56-game_hitting_streak" title="Template:Did you know nominations/Joe DiMaggio's 56-game hitting streak">Joe DiMaggio's 56-game hitting streak</a></li> 
         <li><i>Comment</i>: Please <b>save for July 5</b>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.gov.ky/calendar/public-holidays">Constitution Day</a> in the Cayman Islands <span style="font-size:85%;">(exactly six weeks from now)</span>.</li>
        </ul>
       </dd>
      </dl> 
      <p><small>5x expanded by <a href="/wiki/User:Bloom6132" title="User:Bloom6132">Bloom6132</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Bloom6132" title="User talk:Bloom6132">talk</a>). Self-nominated at 02:50, 23 May 2021 (UTC).</small> </p> 
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <ul>
         <li><a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_question.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol question.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/16px-Symbol_question.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/24px-Symbol_question.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/e/e0/Symbol_question.svg/32px-Symbol_question.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> Always love to see a BOT flag, it's almost guarunteed a spot on <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:DYKSTATS" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:DYKSTATS">WP:DYKSTATS</a>. Reminds I was planning on doing Montserrat's expansion (I assume you have no objection to me nominating that one <span class="template-ping">@<a href="/wiki/User:Bloom6132" title="User:Bloom6132">Bloom6132</a>:</span>?) Nevertheless, here's the review: Date and expansion good. All 3 hooks look good though my preference is for <b>ALT2</b>. QPQ is done and no close paraphrasing. Picture licence is fine. However, just one tiny thing holding it up and that's the merge tag on it but looking at the discussion, it seems to me to be a clear SNOW close in favour of merging. Once that's removed it can be promoted (or would you like me to do it as a NAC?). Please ping me with your response. <span style="text-shadow:grey 0.5em 0.5em 0.6em;"> <b><a href="/wiki/User:The_C_of_E" title="User:The C of E"><span style="color:red;">The C of E </span><span style="color:blue;"> God Save the Queen!</span></a></b> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:The_C_of_E" title="User talk:The C of E"><span style="color:darkblue;">talk</span></a>)</span> 12:56, 23 May 2021 (UTC)</li>
        </ul> 
        <dl>
         <dd>
          <ul>
           <li><span class="template-ping">@<a href="/wiki/User:The_C_of_E" title="User:The C of E">The C of E</a>:</span> Thanks for the review! Feel free to do an NAC –&nbsp;this newly-expanded article covers pretty much everything in <a href="/wiki/List_of_Cayman_Islands_flags" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Cayman Islands flags">List of Cayman Islands flags</a> (other than the old Red Ensign design, which seemed minor enough for me to leave out). —<a href="/wiki/User:Bloom6132" title="User:Bloom6132">Bloom6132</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Bloom6132" title="User talk:Bloom6132">talk</a>) 20:19, 23 May 2021 (UTC)</li>
          </ul> 
          <dl>
           <dd>
            <ul>
             <li><a href="/wiki/File:Symbol_confirmed.svg" class="image"><img alt="Symbol confirmed.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Symbol_confirmed.svg/16px-Symbol_confirmed.svg.png" decoding="async" width="16" height="16" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Symbol_confirmed.svg/24px-Symbol_confirmed.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Symbol_confirmed.svg/32px-Symbol_confirmed.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="180" data-file-height="185"></a> Good to go then. <span style="text-shadow:grey 0.5em 0.5em 0.6em;"> <b><a href="/wiki/User:The_C_of_E" title="User:The C of E"><span style="color:red;">The C of E </span><span style="color:blue;"> God Save the Queen!</span></a></b> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:The_C_of_E" title="User talk:The C of E"><span style="color:darkblue;">talk</span></a>)</span> 20:27, 23 May 2021 (UTC)</li>
